<h3>Terms and Conditions</h3>
<div style="font-size: 13px; line-height: 16px;">
<p>
Only <strong>21 years old and above</strong> is eligible for loan application.
</p>
<p>
To preserve the confidentiality of all information you provide to us we maintain the following Privacy Principles.
</p>
<p>
By clicking "Submit" and providing your personal data, you consent to <strong>our loan providers</strong> contacting you via the telephone and email and permitting to do a search on the Credit Association Singapore (CAS) web portal for the loan application purpose.
</p>
<p>
We only collect personal information that we believe to be relevant and required to understand your financial needs.
</p>
<p>
We will only use any information collected as minimally as possible, mainly to assist us in customising and delivering loan packages that are of interest to our customers.
</p>
<p>
We will not make unsolicited requests for customer information through email or the telephone, unless customers initiate contact with us.
</p>
<p>
We have established strict confidentiality standards for safeguarding information on our customers.
</p>
<p>
Our loan providers will not use or disclose information collected from you other than for the purpose made known to you, authorised by you or required by the Law.
</p>

</div></div></div></div></div><div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-7 fusion-flex-container hundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;--awb-padding-right:0px;--awb-padding-left:0px;--awb-flex-wrap:wrap;" ><div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start fusion-flex-content-wrap" style="width:calc( 100% + 0px ) !important;max-width:calc( 100% + 0px ) !important;margin-left: calc(-0px / 2 );margin-right: calc(-0px / 2 );"><div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-19 fusion_builder_column_1_1 1_1 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-blend:overlay;--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:100%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:0px;--awb-margin-bottom-large:0px;--awb-spacing-left-large:0px;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-spacing-right-medium:0px;--awb-spacing-left-medium:0px;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-spacing-right-small:0px;--awb-spacing-left-small:0px;"><div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column"><div class="fusion-separator fusion-full-width-sep" style="align-self: center;margin-left: auto;margin-right: auto;width:100%;"><div class="fusion-separator-border sep-single sep-solid" style="--awb-height:20px;--awb-amount:20px;border-color:#ecefef;border-top-width:1px;"></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="fusion-fullwidth fullwidth-box fusion-builder-row-8 fusion-flex-container nonhundred-percent-fullwidth non-hundred-percent-height-scrolling" style="--awb-border-radius-top-left:0px;--awb-border-radius-top-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-right:0px;--awb-border-radius-bottom-left:0px;--awb-padding-top:8%;--awb-padding-bottom:28px;--awb-flex-wrap:wrap;" ><div class="fusion-builder-row fusion-row fusion-flex-align-items-flex-start fusion-flex-content-wrap" style="max-width:1227.2px;margin-left: calc(-4% / 2 );margin-right: calc(-4% / 2 );"><div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-20 fusion-flex-column" style="--awb-bg-size:cover;--awb-width-large:60%;--awb-margin-top-large:0px;--awb-spacing-right-large:3.2%;--awb-margin-bottom-large:30px;--awb-spacing-left-large:3.2%;--awb-width-medium:100%;--awb-order-medium:0;--awb-spacing-right-medium:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-medium:1.92%;--awb-width-small:100%;--awb-order-small:0;--awb-spacing-right-small:1.92%;--awb-spacing-left-small:1.92%;"><div class="fusion-column-wrapper fusion-column-has-shadow fusion-flex-justify-content-flex-start fusion-content-layout-column"><div class="fusion-title title fusion-title-17 fusion-sep-none fusion-title-text fusion-title-size-two"><h2 class="fusion-title-heading title-heading-left fusion-responsive-typography-calculated" style="margin:0;--fontSize:46;line-height:1.25;">FAQs You Need to Know</h2></div><div class="accordian fusion-accordian" style="--awb-border-size:1px;--awb-icon-size:14px;--awb-content-font-size:17px;--awb-icon-alignment:left;--awb-hover-color:#f9f9f9;--awb-border-color:#ecefef;--awb-background-color:#ffffff;--awb-divider-color:#ecefef;--awb-divider-hover-color:#ecefef;--awb-icon-color:#ffffff;--awb-title-color:#4d39e9;--awb-content-color:#5c6770;--awb-icon-box-color:#272d3a;--awb-toggle-hover-accent-color:#ffc107;--awb-title-font-family:&quot;Poppins&quot;;--awb-title-font-weight:600;--awb-title-font-style:normal;--awb-title-font-size:21px;--awb-content-font-family:&quot;Karla&quot;;--awb-content-font-style:normal;--awb-content-font-weight:400;"><div class="panel-group fusion-toggle-icon-boxed" id="accordion-1130-1"><div class="fusion-panel panel-default panel-e6edd040e71518df7 fusion-toggle-no-divider fusion-toggle-boxed-mode" style="--awb-title-color:#4d39e9;--awb-content-color:#5c6770;"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title toggle" id="toggle_e6edd040e71518df7"><a aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="e6edd040e71518df7" role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#e6edd040e71518df7" href="#e6edd040e71518df7"><span class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><i class="fa-fusion-box active-icon awb-icon-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa-fusion-box inactive-icon awb-icon-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></span><span class="fusion-toggle-heading">How much I can get or borrow from licensed moneylenders?</span></a></h4></div><div id="e6edd040e71518df7" class="panel-collapse collapse " aria-labelledby="toggle_e6edd040e71518df7"><div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">
<p><span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW210996433 BCX0" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW210996433 BCX0">A secured loan may be requested for any amount. Additionally, your salary </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW210996433 BCX0">determines</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW210996433 BCX0"> how much you may borrow in total with an unsecured loan.</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW210996433 BCX0" data-ccp-props="{"> </span><br />
<b></b></p>
<p><b>For Singaporean or PR </b></p>
<ul>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="34" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="1" data-aria-level="1"><i><span data-contrast="auto">A</span></i><span data-contrast="auto"> maximum of $3000 for those with yearly incomes between $10,000 and $20,000</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="34" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="1" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">A maximum of six times your monthly salary if you make at least $20,000 each year</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
</ul>
<p><b>For Foreigners</b></p>
<ul style="font-weight: 400;">
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="26" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="2" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">A maximum of $1500 for those with yearly incomes under $10,000</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="26" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="3" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">A maximum of $3000 for individuals with annual incomes between $10,000 and $20,000</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="26" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="4" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">A maximum of six times your monthly income for individuals with annual incomes of at least $20,000</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
</ul>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-panel panel-default panel-8776a0cc615e80d7c fusion-toggle-no-divider fusion-toggle-boxed-mode" style="--awb-title-color:#4d39e9;--awb-content-color:#5c6770;"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title toggle" id="toggle_8776a0cc615e80d7c"><a aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="8776a0cc615e80d7c" role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#8776a0cc615e80d7c" href="#8776a0cc615e80d7c"><span class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><i class="fa-fusion-box active-icon awb-icon-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa-fusion-box inactive-icon awb-icon-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></span><span class="fusion-toggle-heading"> How much interest rate can a licensed moneylender charge?</span></a></h4></div><div id="8776a0cc615e80d7c" class="panel-collapse collapse " aria-labelledby="toggle_8776a0cc615e80d7c"><div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">
<p><a href="https://rom.mlaw.gov.sg/information-for-borrowers/guide-to-borrowing-from-licensed-moneylenders-english/#:~:text=What%20are%20the%20interest%20rates,an%20unsecured%20or%20secured%20one." target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span data-contrast="none">Singapore licensed moneylenders may charge up to </span><b><span data-contrast="none">4% monthly interest</span></b></a><span data-contrast="auto"> as of October 1, 2015. </span><b><span data-contrast="auto">Maximum 4% per month of late payment</span></b><span data-contrast="auto">. All loans and income apply.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<p><span data-contrast="auto">The remaining principal determines the monthly interest rate. For instance, the entire principle debt is $12,000, and the payback was $8,000, leaving $4,000. The remaining amount, $4,000, must be charged interest monthly.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<p><span data-contrast="auto">Late monthly payments determine the late interest rate. Another example, if the loan is $10,000, the current payment plan is $2,000, and the remainder is $8,000, the late interest rate will be levied on $2,000.</span></p>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-panel panel-default panel-6ecd1275fc3d58919 fusion-toggle-no-divider fusion-toggle-boxed-mode" style="--awb-title-color:#4d39e9;--awb-content-color:#5c6770;"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title toggle" id="toggle_6ecd1275fc3d58919"><a aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="6ecd1275fc3d58919" role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#6ecd1275fc3d58919" href="#6ecd1275fc3d58919"><span class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><i class="fa-fusion-box active-icon awb-icon-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa-fusion-box inactive-icon awb-icon-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></span><span class="fusion-toggle-heading">What factors should I consider prior to obtaining a loan?</span></a></h4></div><div id="6ecd1275fc3d58919" class="panel-collapse collapse " aria-labelledby="toggle_6ecd1275fc3d58919"><div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">
<p><span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW254718661 BCX0" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW254718661 BCX0">You will be legally responsible if you take out a loan. </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW254718661 BCX0">In order to</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW254718661 BCX0"> obtain one, you need </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW254718661 BCX0">take into account</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW254718661 BCX0"> the following:</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW254718661 BCX0" data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<ul>
<li><strong>Check for Other Alternatives.</strong> <span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW131802011 BCX0" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW131802011 BCX0">There are other choices than </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW131802011 BCX0">licens</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW131802011 BCX0">ed moneylenders that may </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW131802011 BCX0">assist</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW131802011 BCX0"> you with your financial demands. Another </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW131802011 BCX0">option</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW131802011 BCX0"> is to apply for financial aid from various government agencies.</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW131802011 BCX0" data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li><strong>Note of Contract.</strong> <span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW233501990 BCX0" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW233501990 BCX0">You must abide by the terms and conditions set out in the Note of Contract with the licensed money lender. Settlements in court might result from failure to comply.</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW233501990 BCX0" data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li><strong>Ability to Repay.</strong> <span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW268042022 BCX0" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW268042022 BCX0">Make sure you have examined your financial situation and understand your </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW268042022 BCX0">capacity</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW268042022 BCX0"> to repay before taking out a loan from a moneylender. Your income and your financial demands must be </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW268042022 BCX0">taken into account</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW268042022 BCX0">. Keep in mind that making </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW268042022 BCX0">late payments</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW268042022 BCX0"> will result in both late interest and a late payback charge. It is advised that you borrow less money than you make and that you only </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW268042022 BCX0">utilise</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW268042022 BCX0"> it for emergency requirements. Never spend money on lavish expenditures.</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW268042022 BCX0" data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li><strong>Full Understanding of the Contract.</strong> <span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW57322261 BCX0" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW57322261 BCX0">You, as the borrower, must fully </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW57322261 BCX0">comprehend</span> <span class="NormalTextRun SCXW57322261 BCX0">all of</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW57322261 BCX0"> the contract&#8217;s terms and conditions. Consider the following: the repayment timeline, interest rate, and fees. You must confirm, as required by law, that the lenders have adequately described the Note of Contract. They must also </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW57322261 BCX0">provide</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW57322261 BCX0"> a copy of the agreement to you.</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW57322261 BCX0" data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li><strong>Caveats on Property.</strong> <span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW159261104 BCX0" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW159261104 BCX0">You must carefully read the Note of Contract. Make sure you are fully aware of the implications of placing </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW159261104 BCX0">a </span></span><a class="Hyperlink SCXW159261104 BCX0" href="https://singaporelegaladvice.com/law-articles/lodge-caveat-property-singapore/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span class="FieldRange SCXW159261104 BCX0"><span class="TextRun Highlight Underlined SCXW159261104 BCX0" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="none"><span class="NormalTextRun CommentStart CommentHighlightPipeRest CommentHighlightRest SCXW159261104 BCX0" data-ccp-charstyle="Hyperlink">caveat</span><span class="NormalTextRun CommentHighlightRest SCXW159261104 BCX0" data-ccp-charstyle="Hyperlink"> on your properties</span></span></span></a><span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW159261104 BCX0" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun CommentHighlightPipeRest SCXW159261104 BCX0">. Keep in mind that if moneylenders place </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW159261104 BCX0">a caveat</span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW159261104 BCX0"> on your real estate, you could not get any of the selling profits until you completely repay the debt. As a result, you must carefully read the conditions before signing.</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW159261104 BCX0" data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li><strong>Search for Other Moneylenders.</strong> <span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW255104152 BCX0" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW255104152 BCX0">You must choose a moneylender whose terms and conditions best fit your financial demands since they differ among them. Choose the one with beneficial terms as well.</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW255104152 BCX0" data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
</ul>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-panel panel-default panel-c622e9861ee6005a9 fusion-toggle-no-divider fusion-toggle-boxed-mode" style="--awb-title-color:#4d39e9;--awb-content-color:#5c6770;"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title toggle" id="toggle_c622e9861ee6005a9"><a aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="c622e9861ee6005a9" role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#c622e9861ee6005a9" href="#c622e9861ee6005a9"><span class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><i class="fa-fusion-box active-icon awb-icon-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa-fusion-box inactive-icon awb-icon-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></span><span class="fusion-toggle-heading">What are the fees that a licensed moneylender can charge?</span></a></h4></div><div id="c622e9861ee6005a9" class="panel-collapse collapse " aria-labelledby="toggle_c622e9861ee6005a9"><div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">
<p><span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW101485862 BCX0" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW101485862 BCX0">Moneylenders may only charge the following fees as of October 1, 2015:</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW101485862 BCX0" data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<ul>
<li><strong>a maximum of $60</strong> for each month of failure to repay a loan;</li>
<li><strong>a maximum of 10%</strong> of the principal loan from the time the loan was granted or known as an administrative fee; and</li>
<li><strong>legal cost awarded by the court</strong> for the loan recovery for each successful loan claim by a licensed moneylender</li>
</ul>
<p><span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW27396053 BCX0" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW27396053 BCX0">Keep in mind that the total fees cannot be more than the loan&#8217;s principal amount. For instance, the overall fees, including interest rates, late interest, late repayment fees, and administrative fees, cannot exceed $10,000, for instance, if the principal loan is $10,000.</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW27396053 BCX0" data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-panel panel-default panel-c85ff6ab4f4ea9b93 fusion-toggle-no-divider fusion-toggle-boxed-mode" style="--awb-title-color:#4d39e9;--awb-content-color:#5c6770;"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title toggle" id="toggle_c85ff6ab4f4ea9b93"><a aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="c85ff6ab4f4ea9b93" role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#c85ff6ab4f4ea9b93" href="#c85ff6ab4f4ea9b93"><span class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><i class="fa-fusion-box active-icon awb-icon-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa-fusion-box inactive-icon awb-icon-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></span><span class="fusion-toggle-heading">How to verify if a moneylender is a licensed one or not?</span></a></h4></div><div id="c85ff6ab4f4ea9b93" class="panel-collapse collapse " aria-labelledby="toggle_c85ff6ab4f4ea9b93"><div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">
<p><span data-contrast="auto">A licensed moneylender is included in the Ministry of Law&#8217;s </span><a href="https://rom.mlaw.gov.sg/information-for-borrowers/list-of-licensed-moneylenders-in-singapore/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span data-contrast="none">monthly updated Registry of Moneylenders list</span></a><span data-contrast="auto">, which is available as a PDF file.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<p><span data-contrast="auto">Despite a moneylender&#8217;s licence, be cautious and watch out for the following dishonest actions:</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<ul>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="29" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="1" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Making threats and using abusive language</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="29" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="2" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Requesting your SIngPass Log-in information</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="29" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="3" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Keeping your NRIC card and identification on you, such as your driver&#8217;s licence, ATM card, and so on.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="29" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="4" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Have you sign a loan agreement that is either blank or insufficient</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="29" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="5" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Failed to provide you with a copy of this contract and failed to explain the terms and conditions included in the Note of Contract.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="29" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="5" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Approve a loan over the phone, over email, or by text message rather than following the law. Before disbursing a loan, the lender must personally meet the borrower in accordance with the legislation; and</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="29" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="5" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Withdrew from a principal loan a sum that was not covered by the administrative charge</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
</ul>
<p><span data-contrast="auto">The Ah-long hotline at 1800-2255-529 must be contacted about the unfair practises listed above. Contact the Registry of Moneylenders and have your company name, licence number, and phone number handy.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<p>To learn further about unlicensed moneylenders you can <a href="https://www.police.gov.sg/resources/prevent-crime/unlicensed-moneylending/loansharking-situation-in-singapore" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">click here</a>.</p>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-panel panel-default panel-e4d0cdaec28a6df8f fusion-toggle-no-divider fusion-toggle-boxed-mode" style="--awb-title-color:#4d39e9;--awb-content-color:#5c6770;"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title toggle" id="toggle_e4d0cdaec28a6df8f"><a aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="e4d0cdaec28a6df8f" role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#e4d0cdaec28a6df8f" href="#e4d0cdaec28a6df8f"><span class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><i class="fa-fusion-box active-icon awb-icon-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa-fusion-box inactive-icon awb-icon-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></span><span class="fusion-toggle-heading">How to tell the difference of an advertisement of a Licensed moneylender from an unlicensed one?</span></a></h4></div><div id="e4d0cdaec28a6df8f" class="panel-collapse collapse " aria-labelledby="toggle_e4d0cdaec28a6df8f"><div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">
<p><span data-contrast="auto">A licensed lender of money may only use the following media to advertise:</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<ul>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="30" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="1" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Business or consumer directories, either online or offline.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="30" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="2" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Registered Website Address</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="30" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="3" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Within the office premises</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
</ul>
<p><span data-contrast="auto">Outside of the three (3) channels, advertising is prohibited. This is one of the criteria that separates a licensed individual from one who is not.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<p><span data-contrast="auto">An unlicensed moneylender may use fliers, email, SMS, and social media sites like Facebook and WhatsApp to promote. So be careful and don&#8217;t answer them. You may file a complaint by calling 1800-2255-529 or using their </span><a href="https://www.mlaw.gov.sg/eservices/enquiry/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span data-contrast="none">contact form</span></a><span data-contrast="auto">.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
</div></div></div></div></div><div class="accordian fusion-accordian" style="--awb-border-size:1px;--awb-icon-size:14px;--awb-content-font-size:17px;--awb-icon-alignment:left;--awb-hover-color:#f9f9f9;--awb-border-color:#ecefef;--awb-background-color:#ffffff;--awb-divider-color:#ecefef;--awb-divider-hover-color:#ecefef;--awb-icon-color:#ffffff;--awb-title-color:#4d39e9;--awb-content-color:#5c6770;--awb-icon-box-color:#272d3a;--awb-toggle-hover-accent-color:#ffc107;--awb-title-font-family:&quot;Poppins&quot;;--awb-title-font-weight:600;--awb-title-font-style:normal;--awb-title-font-size:21px;--awb-content-font-family:&quot;Karla&quot;;--awb-content-font-style:normal;--awb-content-font-weight:400;"><div class="panel-group fusion-toggle-icon-boxed" id="accordion-1130-2"><div class="fusion-panel panel-default panel-414f5d7beff4a58ef fusion-toggle-no-divider fusion-toggle-boxed-mode" style="--awb-title-color:#4d39e9;--awb-content-color:#5c6770;"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title toggle" id="toggle_414f5d7beff4a58ef"><a aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="414f5d7beff4a58ef" role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#414f5d7beff4a58ef" href="#414f5d7beff4a58ef"><span class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><i class="fa-fusion-box active-icon awb-icon-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa-fusion-box inactive-icon awb-icon-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></span><span class="fusion-toggle-heading">When securing a loan, can I depend on the content of the advertisement?</span></a></h4></div><div id="414f5d7beff4a58ef" class="panel-collapse collapse " aria-labelledby="toggle_414f5d7beff4a58ef"><div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">
<p><span class="TextRun Highlight SCXW129524646 BCX0" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW129524646 BCX0">Relying just on the advertisement&#8217;s substance is insufficient. There is not much information provided. You may get more information by calling or visiting the </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW129524646 BCX0">licensed </span><span class="NormalTextRun SCXW129524646 BCX0">money</span> <span class="NormalTextRun SCXW129524646 BCX0">lender&#8217;s office.</span></span><span class="EOP SCXW129524646 BCX0" data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-panel panel-default panel-b146dbfeaa55fe228 fusion-toggle-no-divider fusion-toggle-boxed-mode" style="--awb-title-color:#4d39e9;--awb-content-color:#5c6770;"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title toggle" id="toggle_b146dbfeaa55fe228"><a aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="b146dbfeaa55fe228" role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#b146dbfeaa55fe228" href="#b146dbfeaa55fe228"><span class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><i class="fa-fusion-box active-icon awb-icon-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa-fusion-box inactive-icon awb-icon-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></span><span class="fusion-toggle-heading">What factors do I need to consider when standing as a surety for the loan?</span></a></h4></div><div id="b146dbfeaa55fe228" class="panel-collapse collapse " aria-labelledby="toggle_b146dbfeaa55fe228"><div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">
<p><span data-contrast="auto">The following are the considerations you should keep in mind while acting as a surety:</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<ul>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="31" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="1" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Keep in mind your obligation</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="31" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="2" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">When the loan is approved, a copy of the Note of Contract must be present.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="31" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="3" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">The licensed lender clearly stated the Note of Contract.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="31" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="4" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">The terms of the contract are also explained</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="31" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="4" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">A moneylender can&#8217;t take away your NRIC or personal identification documents; and</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="31" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="4" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">The moneylender must not request sensitive information, such as a SingPass account, an email address, or access to online banking.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
</ul>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-panel panel-default panel-da2601c86b6bfefab fusion-toggle-no-divider fusion-toggle-boxed-mode" style="--awb-title-color:#4d39e9;--awb-content-color:#5c6770;"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title toggle" id="toggle_da2601c86b6bfefab"><a aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="da2601c86b6bfefab" role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#da2601c86b6bfefab" href="#da2601c86b6bfefab"><span class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><i class="fa-fusion-box active-icon awb-icon-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa-fusion-box inactive-icon awb-icon-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></span><span class="fusion-toggle-heading">What should I do after a licensed moneylender granted me a loan?</span></a></h4></div><div id="da2601c86b6bfefab" class="panel-collapse collapse " aria-labelledby="toggle_da2601c86b6bfefab"><div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">
<p><span data-contrast="auto">When you get a loan, be careful to follow these rules:</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<ul>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="32" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="3" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">You must ensure that licensed moneylenders provide the correct amount of total principal loans with a maximum administrative charge reduction of 10%.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="32" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="3" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Pay promptly. Avoid making late payments to avoid paying late interest and fees.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="32" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="3" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Whenever you make a repayment, make sure the date, name, and amount are all spelt correctly on the receipt.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="32" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="3" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Ensure that you will get a copy of the statement of account for your loans every January and July. Do not forget to confirm the accuracy of your information, including the name, amount, and date.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
<li data-leveltext="" data-font="Symbol" data-listid="32" data-list-defn-props="{" aria-setsize="-1" data-aria-posinset="3" data-aria-level="1"><span data-contrast="auto">Keep copies of your account statements and receipts carefully; they will serve as evidence of all your payments.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></li>
</ul>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-panel panel-default panel-8a7f6867c18666ef4 fusion-toggle-no-divider fusion-toggle-boxed-mode" style="--awb-title-color:#4d39e9;--awb-content-color:#5c6770;"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title toggle" id="toggle_8a7f6867c18666ef4"><a aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="8a7f6867c18666ef4" role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#8a7f6867c18666ef4" href="#8a7f6867c18666ef4"><span class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><i class="fa-fusion-box active-icon awb-icon-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa-fusion-box inactive-icon awb-icon-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></span><span class="fusion-toggle-heading">How to report a moneylender against unfair and illegal practices/contract?</span></a></h4></div><div id="8a7f6867c18666ef4" class="panel-collapse collapse " aria-labelledby="toggle_8a7f6867c18666ef4"><div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">
<p><a href="https://rom.mlaw.gov.sg/contact-us/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><span data-contrast="none">Call the Registry of Moneylenders at </span><b><span data-contrast="none">1800-2255-529</span></b></a><span data-contrast="auto"> to file a complaint about unfair lending practises. Your complaint will be taken seriously, and the Registry will look into it. You may also need to provide them any pertinent papers and data. You can also be requested to appear for an interview with a representative of the Registry.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<p><span data-contrast="auto">According to the Consumer Protection (Fair Trading) Act, you may file a lawsuit via the Small Claims Tribunal or the Court if an inquiry reveals that a moneylender is using unfair practises.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
</div></div></div><div class="fusion-panel panel-default panel-419820fd7cc7b0458 fusion-toggle-no-divider fusion-toggle-boxed-mode" style="--awb-title-color:#4d39e9;--awb-content-color:#5c6770;"><div class="panel-heading"><h4 class="panel-title toggle" id="toggle_419820fd7cc7b0458"><a aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="419820fd7cc7b0458" role="button" data-toggle="collapse" data-target="#419820fd7cc7b0458" href="#419820fd7cc7b0458"><span class="fusion-toggle-icon-wrapper" aria-hidden="true"><i class="fa-fusion-box active-icon awb-icon-minus" aria-hidden="true"></i><i class="fa-fusion-box inactive-icon awb-icon-plus" aria-hidden="true"></i></span><span class="fusion-toggle-heading">Can the Registry of Moneylenders help me in negotiation with a licensed moneylender when I have financial problems and cannot repay the moneylender?</span></a></h4></div><div id="419820fd7cc7b0458" class="panel-collapse collapse " aria-labelledby="toggle_419820fd7cc7b0458"><div class="panel-body toggle-content fusion-clearfix">
<p><span data-contrast="auto">The Registry of Moneylenders is unable to assist you in this situation since your dispute concerns a private contract or agreement between you and the moneylender.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<p><span data-contrast="auto">You may get assistance from social service organisations if you&#8217;re having financial problems. They will educate you on basic credit management, help you get counselling, and even help you acquire a repayment plan.</span><span data-ccp-props="{"> </span></p>
<ul>

<p><em><span class="TextRun BCX0 SCXW162787993" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun BCX0 SCXW162787993">*Credit Counselling Singapore may also </span></span><span class="TextRun BCX0 SCXW162787993" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun BCX0 SCXW162787993">involve</span></span><span class="TextRun BCX0 SCXW162787993" lang="EN-US" xml:lang="EN-US" data-contrast="auto"><span class="NormalTextRun BCX0 SCXW162787993"> in handling debt cases with banks.</span></span><span class="EOP BCX0 SCXW162787993" data-ccp-props="{"> </span></em></p>
</div></div></div></div></div></div></div><div class="fusion-layout-column fusion_builder_column fusion-builder-column-21 fusion-flex-column"
